The cafeteria at night is also strongly recommended, with a rich variety, and there are great discounts for the elderly according to their age, such as small seafood steaming, shabu-shabu, grilled skewers, barbecue, etc.! When we checked out and left, they brought us a bag of water, snacks, wipes, and masks. Anyway, everything is very good! If you don't require a room with a sea view, Bliss is definitely the first choice in Weihai!
